Foreign Important Telegrams

May 1st Labor Day Commemoration

Minor Disturbances Occur Around the World

Moscow Celebrates Grandly

Unique America: Tranquility and Peace

Reuters News Agency, Tokyo, 1st - In Tokyo, the Labor Day demonstration and parade proceeded as scheduled despite the continuous spring rain. It involved tens of thousands of male and female laborers, an unprecedented number since Japan began celebrating Labor Day. As the event was dispersing, a group of union allies threw stones at the police, causing a major riot. Sixteen people from both sides were seriously or lightly injured, and 770 people were detained, of whom 202 have been released.

Associated Press, New York, 1st - Labor Day in the United States was peaceful and tranquil. Although there were parades and speeches in major cities, strict precautions prevented any incidents.

Reuters News Agency, London, 1st - Judging from reports from around the world, the disturbances on this year's May Day Labor Day were fewer than in previous years. In Munich, Germany, the Communist Party attempted to disrupt May Day celebrations by throwing stones at the police, but they were dispersed by police batons. Seven police officers were injured. In Berlin, a Communist Party member shot and killed a police officer. The National Socialist Party and the Socialist Party clashed in front of Berlin University. The Socialist Party hung a Soviet Russian red flag on the roof, but it was eventually torn down. There were no other serious conflicts. In the Austrian capital, 8,000 people participated in demonstrations, but order was maintained. In the capital of Belgium, although there was Communist Party agitation, no disturbances to peace occurred. In Queensland, Australia, gatherings were prohibited, but some people in Brisbane attempted to hold demonstrations, resulting in the arrest of twenty people by the police. In Johannesburg, South Africa, after the May Day commemoration, a crowd of a thousand people attempted to destroy the new Carlton Hotel and the Rand Club. A large number of police arrived by vehicle to stop the rioters and arrested seven Europeans and two Fijians. In Częstochowa, Poland, a Communist Party demonstration resulted in two deaths and several injuries. Elsewhere, things were generally peaceful. The new Spanish government allowed May Day celebrations to be held in Madrid. Crowds gathered in front of Prime Minister Zamora's residence. Zamora and his cabinet members appeared on the balcony, and the crowd cheered and presented a petition requesting approval for those aged 21 and over to have the right to vote, ratification of the eight-hour workday convention, and relief for unemployment. However, Barcelona was not so peaceful. When a trade union delegation met with local authorities at the local administrative office, gunshots suddenly rang out from the crowd outside the office, resulting in one police officer dead and two seriously injured, and twelve civilians injured, including three with serious injuries. Officials on the balcony of the administrative office loudly urged the public to maintain order, and a large contingent of police arrived to persuade the crowd to disperse. The cause of the shooting is unknown. All parts of France were peaceful, but in Paris, some people distributing inflammatory leaflets were arrested by the police, totaling forty people. In the suburbs of Paris, a clash between the Communist Party and the police resulted in several demonstrators and four police officers being injured, but the injuries were minor. In Bombay, India, three thousand strikers held demonstrations, but there were no disturbances. All parts of England were peaceful, with only a slight dispute between police and the public in Hyde Park in the evening, resulting in one police officer injured and four people arrested.

National News Agency, Moscow, 1st - The Soviet Union throughout its territory attaches great importance to Labor Day. Every year there are military reviews and workers' parades, etc. This year is the same, but due to adhering to the Five-Year Plan, work throughout the country has not been suspended. Those who participate in the parade are workers who are usually off work, accounting for one-fifth of the total. When the factories release workers, the parade expands. In addition to being covered in red flags, the streets of Moscow are decorated with various slogans and satirical anti-communist cartoons. Parades from all over gathered in Red Square, where Soviet leaders such as Stalin stood high on Lenin's Mausoleum to review the parades and naval and military exercises.

Muslims Do Not Slaughter Cattle During Eid al-Adha

Spirit of Cooperation Among Indian Muslims

National News Agency, Bombay, 30th - The Indian Muslim authorities issued an order to Muslims that this year during Eid al-Adha, instead of slaughtering calves, they should slaughter foals, lambs, and camels for sacrifice to avoid hurting the feelings of Indian Hindus who revere cattle. Indian newspapers, in light of the recent Kanpur tragedy in which more than two thousand people were killed due to trivial disputes between followers of the two religions, highly commend the Muslim leaders for being able to set aside their prejudices and change old practices by issuing this order, considering it a very important move and the first such unusual event in Indian history. They are delighted and regard it as a good omen for India's prosperous and bright future.

Romanian King Orders Dissolution of Parliament

General Election to be Held in Early June

Reuters News Agency, Bucharest, 30th - King Carol of Romania's interference in state affairs has caused tension in political circles. Last night, there were people in the streets of Bucharest shouting "Long live Spain!" but there were also those shouting "Long live the King!" Today, the Senate announced that the government's policies include restoring the privileges of the monarchy, which greatly angered the public. Subsequently, it announced the King's order to dissolve Parliament and hold a general election in early June, causing a great uproar. It is expected that the competition in this election will be very fierce.

Catalonia Province of Spain Organizes Independent Cabinet

Macià Disregards His Previous Words

National News Agency, Madrid, 30th - Although the dispute between mainland Spain and Catalonia Province had been eased as a result of personal mediation by the Provisional Government's Prime Minister Zamora, Catalonia Province today organized a cabinet, with Macià himself serving as Prime Minister. This move has now aroused a complete backlash in Madrid's public opinion because Macià had previously promised not to take any actions that would harm the credibility of the Madrid Provisional Government. This organization of an independent cabinet is clearly reneging on his previous promise.

France's Memorandum in Response to the German-Austrian Customs Union Delivered to Various Countries

National News Agency, Paris, 30th - Foreign Minister Briand's response to the German-Austrian customs union was passed by the Cabinet on Wednesday and, after revisions by the relevant states, was telegraphed to various national capitals tonight and formally delivered to various national governments by French diplomatic representatives. The memorandum is divided into two sections. The first section discusses methods for the sale of surplus grain from Eastern and Southern European countries. It also mentions the economic assistance that should be provided to certain countries, such as Austria, so that it will no longer need to conclude a customs treaty with Germany. The date of publication of the memorandum has not yet been determined.

Japan Prepares to Reduce the Army

Savings Used to Increase Armament Strength

Reuters, Tokyo, 2nd - According to a newspaper report, although confirmation has not yet been obtained, the army authorities have agreed to reduce the national army from approximately 210,000 to 180,000, which would save 12 million yuan to be used to increase the strength of army armaments.

Important News

Full Text of the Draft Provisional Constitution for the Period of Political Tutelage

Passed by the Central Provisional Plenary Session

The Provisional Plenary Session of the Central Executive and Supervisory Committees convened a meeting on the afternoon of the 2nd and revised and passed the draft Provisional Constitution of the Republic of China for the Period of Political Tutelage. The full text is as follows:

The National Government, based on the Three Principles of the People and the Five-Power Constitution established by the revolution, aims to build the Republic of China. As it transitions from the period of military rule to the period of political tutelage, it is appropriate to promulgate a Provisional Constitution for common observance, with the goal of facilitating the handover of political power and entrusting it to a popularly elected government. Hereby, in accordance with the will of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the founder of the Republic of China and the leader of the Kuomintang, a National Assembly is convened in the capital, and the National Assembly resolves the Provisional Constitution of the Republic of China for the Period of Political Tutelage as follows:

Chapter I: General Principles

Article 1: The territory of the Republic of China consists of the provinces, Mongolia, and Tibet.

Article 2: The sovereignty of the Republic of China belongs to all the citizens. All those who legally possess the nationality of the Republic of China are citizens of the Republic of China.

Article 3: The Republic of China shall forever be a unified republic.

Article 4: The national flag of the Republic of China shall be red with a white sun in a blue sky in the upper left corner.

Article 5: The capital of the Republic of China shall be Nanjing.

Chapter II: Rights and Obligations of the People

Article 6: Citizens of the Republic of China shall be equal before the law, regardless of gender, race, religion, or class.

Article 7: Citizens of the Republic of China shall, in accordance with Article 8 of the Outline of National Reconstruction, enjoy the rights of election, recall, initiative, and referendum in fully autonomous counties, as stipulated in Article 9 of the Outline of National Reconstruction.

Article 8: No person shall be arrested, detained, interrogated, or punished except in accordance with the law. In the event that a person is arrested or detained on suspicion of a crime, the agency executing the arrest or detention shall transfer the person to the judicial authorities for interrogation within twenty-four hours at the latest. The person or others may request a writ of habeas corpus within twenty-four hours in accordance with the law.

Article 9: No person shall be subject to military trial except for those currently serving in the military, and only in accordance with the law.

Article 10: The domicile of a person shall not be entered, searched, or sealed except in accordance with the law.

Article 11: The people shall have freedom of religious belief.

Article 12: The people shall have freedom of movement, which shall not be suspended or restricted except in accordance with the law.

Article 13: The people shall have freedom of correspondence and telegraphic communication, which shall not be suspended or restricted except in accordance with the law.

Article 14: The people shall have freedom of association and assembly, which shall not be suspended or restricted except in accordance with the law.

Article 15: The people shall have freedom of speech and publication, which shall not be suspended or restricted except in accordance with the law.

Article 16: The property of the people shall not be confiscated or seized except in accordance with the law.

Article 17: The exercise of the right to own property by the people shall be protected by law, to the extent that it does not harm public interests.

Article 18: The property of the people may be requisitioned or expropriated in accordance with the law when necessary for public interest.

Article 19: The people shall have the right to inherit property in accordance with the law.

Article 20: The people shall have the right to petition.

Article 21: The people shall have the right to bring suit in court in accordance with the law.

Article 22: The people shall have the right to file administrative appeals and administrative lawsuits in accordance with the law.

Article 23: The people shall have the right to take examinations in accordance with the law.

Article 24: The people shall have the right to hold public office in accordance with the law.

Article 25: The people shall have the obligation to pay taxes in accordance with the law.

Article 26: The people shall have the obligation to perform military service and corvée in accordance with the law.

Article 27: The people shall have the obligation to obey the lawful execution of duties by public authorities.

Chapter III: Outline of Political Tutelage

Article 28: The political outline and its implementation during the period of political tutelage shall be in accordance with the provisions of the Outline of National Reconstruction.

Article 29: Local self-government shall be promoted in accordance with the provisions of the Outline of National Reconstruction and the Law on the Implementation of Local Self-Government.

Article 30: During the period of political tutelage, the National Congress of the Kuomintang shall represent the National Assembly in exercising the central governing power. When the National Congress of the Kuomintang is not in session, its functions shall be exercised by the Central Executive Committee of the Kuomintang.

Article 31: The exercise of the four political rights of election, recall, initiative, and referendum shall be guided by the National Government.

Article 32: The five powers of governance—executive, legislative, judicial, examination, and control—shall be exercised by the National Government.

Chapter IV: People's Livelihood

Article 33: In order to develop the people's livelihood, the state shall encourage or protect the productive enterprises of the people.

Article 34: In order to develop the rural economy, improve the lives of farmers, and increase the welfare of tenant farmers, the state shall actively implement the following measures: (1) Reclaim wasteland throughout the country and develop agricultural irrigation. (2) Establish agricultural financial institutions and encourage rural cooperative enterprises. (3) Implement a warehousing system to prevent famine and ensure sufficient food for the people. (4) Develop agricultural education, emphasize scientific experimentation, promote agricultural extension, and increase agricultural production. (5) Encourage local construction of rural roads to facilitate the transportation of products.

Article 35: The people shall have the freedom to choose their occupations and businesses, but the state may restrict or prohibit those that harm the public interest by law.

Article 36: The people shall have the freedom to conclude contracts, which shall be protected by law, to the extent that they do not harm public interests or good morals.

Article 37: The people may, in accordance with the law, organize vocational groups to improve economic life and promote labor-management cooperation.

Article 38: Labor and management should develop productive enterprises on the principle of coordination and mutual benefit.

Article 39: In order to improve the living conditions of workers, the state shall implement laws and regulations to protect workers. Women and children engaged in labor shall be given special protection according to their age and physical condition.

Article 40: In order to prevent and relieve farmers and workers who are unable to work due to injury, illness, disability, or old age, the state shall implement a labor insurance system.

Article 41: In order to promote the development of the national economy, the state shall promote various cooperative enterprises.

Article 42: The state may adjust or restrict the production, sale, and prices of necessities for the people's livelihood.

Article 43: Usurious loans and exorbitant rents for the use of real estate shall be prohibited by law.

Article 44: The state shall provide appropriate relief to current military personnel who become disabled due to their service.

Chapter V: National Education

Article 45: The Three Principles of the People shall be the fundamental principles of education in the Republic of China.

Article 46: Equal opportunities in education shall be provided for both men and women.

Article 47: All public and private educational institutions throughout the country shall be subject to state supervision and shall be responsible for promoting the national education policies established by the state.

Article 48: All children who have reached school age shall receive compulsory education. The details shall be determined by law.

Article 49: The state shall provide adult literacy education to people who have not received compulsory education.

Page 10

Article 50: The central and local governments shall raise the necessary funds for education and shall protect the independence of educational funds by law.

Article 51: The state shall reward and protect school teachers and staff who have excellent performance and have been in their positions for a long time.

Article 52: All public and private schools throughout the country shall set up free places to reward students with excellent character and academic performance who are unable to afford further education.

Article 53: The state shall reward and protect academic and technological research and inventions.

Article 54: The state shall protect or preserve historical relics, cultural artifacts, and artistic antiquities.

Chapter VI: Central and Local Powers

Article 55: The powers of the central and local governments shall be based on the principle of equitable distribution of powers as stipulated in Article 17 of the Outline of National Reconstruction.

Article 56: Local governments may enact local regulations within the scope of their authority, but those that conflict with central laws and regulations shall be invalid.

Article 57: The division of taxes between the central government and local governments shall be determined by law.

Article 58: The central government may, in order to eliminate the evils of the following items in local taxation, establish general rules to restrict them by law: (1) Harming social public interests. (2) Harming the source of central government revenue. (3) Double taxation. (4) Hindering transportation. (5) Unfair taxation for the benefit of one locality on goods imported from other localities. (6) Local transit taxes.

Article 59: Patents, monopolies, and concessions for industry and commerce shall belong to the central government.

Article 60: When a province reaches the stage of constitutional government, the powers of the central and local governments shall be specified in detail by law in accordance with the Outline of National Reconstruction.

Chapter VII: Organization of the Government

Section 1: Central System

Article 61: The National Government shall exercise the governing power of the Republic of China.

Article 62: The National Government shall command the army, navy, and air force.

Article 63: The National Government shall exercise the power to declare war, make peace, and conclude treaties.

Article 64: The National Government shall grant general amnesties, special pardons, and reductions of sentences, and shall restore rights.

Article 65: The National Government shall confer honors.

Article 66: The National Government shall establish the Executive Yuan, the Legislative Yuan, the Judicial Yuan, the Examination Yuan, and Control Yuan, as well as various ministries and commissions.

Article 67: The National Government shall have one Chairman and a number of members, who shall be elected by the Central Executive Committee of the Kuomintang. The number of members shall be determined separately by law.

Article 68: The Chairman of the National Government shall represent the National Government internally and externally.

Article 69: The heads of the various Yuans, ministries, and commissions shall be appointed and dismissed by the National Government in accordance with the law upon the recommendation of the Chairman of the National Government.

Article 70: Laws shall be promulgated and orders shall be issued by the Chairman of the National Government in accordance with the law.

Article 71: The various ministries and commissions may issue orders in accordance with the law.

Article 72: The organization of the National Government and the various Yuans, ministries, and commissions shall be determined by law.

Section 2: Local System

Article 73: Each province shall have a provincial government under the direction of the central government, which shall comprehensively manage the administrative affairs of the entire province. Its organization shall be determined by law.

Article 74: When a province reaches the stage of constitutional government in accordance with the provisions of Article 16 of the Outline of National Reconstruction, the National Representatives Assembly may elect a provincial governor.

Article 75: The system for areas in Mongolia and Tibet that have not been established as provinces may be determined separately by law based on local conditions.

Article 76: Each county shall have a county government under the direction of the provincial government, which shall comprehensively manage the administrative affairs of the entire county. Its organization shall be determined by law.

Article 77: Each county shall promptly organize a county self-government preparatory committee to carry out the preparatory matters stipulated in Article 8 of the Outline of National Reconstruction. The organization of the county self-government preparatory committee shall be determined by law.

Article 78: In areas where industry and commerce are prosperous, the population is concentrated, or there are other special circumstances, various municipalities may be established in accordance with the provisions of law. Their organization shall be determined by law.

Chapter VIII: Supplementary Provisions

Article 79: The power to interpret this Provisional Constitution shall be exercised by the Provisional Constitution Interpretation Committee. The organization of the Provisional Constitution Interpretation Committee shall be determined by law.

Article 80: The draft constitution shall be based on the Outline of National Reconstruction and the achievements of both the period of political tutelage and the period of constitutional government, and shall be deliberated by the Legislative Yuan. It shall be publicized to the public at any time in order to be adopted and implemented when the time comes.

Article 81: When more than half of the provinces in the country reach the stage of constitutional government, that is, the stage when local self-government in the entire province is fully established, the National Government shall immediately convene a National Assembly to determine the constitution and promulgate it.

Article 82: This Provisional Constitution shall take effect from the date of its promulgation.

Provisional Plenary Session of the Central Executive and Supervisory Committees

▲Revised Draft Provisional Constitution

▲Passed Proposals for the National Assembly

The Provisional Plenary Session of the Central Executive and Supervisory Committee was held at the Central Party Headquarters from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM on the 1st to discuss the draft Provisional Constitution and continued in session from 3:00 PM to 5:00 PM. The attending committee members included Chiang Kai-shek, Dai Jitao, Ye Chucang, Wu Tiecheng, Yu Youren, Soong Tzu-wen, He Chengjun, Shao Yuanchong, Zhu Jiahua, Zhang Qun, Liu Zhi, Yang Shuzhuang, Zhou Qigang, Chen Lifu, Chen Zhaoying, Liu Jiwen, Liu Luyin, Ding Weifen, Zeng Yangfu, Fang Juehui, Wang Zhengting, Zhang Zhen, Kong Xiangxi, Liu Wendao, Lu Diping, Zhang Daofan, Miao Bin, Gui Chongji, Yu Jingtang, Jiao Yitang, Miao Peicheng, Cheng Tianfang, Ke Xing'e, Wu Jingheng, Zhang Renjie, Cai Yuanpei, Zhang Ji, Shao Lizi, Li Yuying, Enhe Batu, Chu Minyi, and Chen Bulei. Zhang Xueliang attended as an observer. Dai Jitao chaired the meeting. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Revised and passed the draft Provisional Constitution. (2) Appointed Wu Jingheng, Li Yuying, Zhang Ji, Wu Tiecheng, Yu Youren, Liu Luyin, Chen Bulei, Chen Lifu, and Shao Lizi as the nine members of the committee to review proposals for the National Assembly. (3) The meeting will continue at 3:00 PM tomorrow (the 2nd).

The Provisional Plenary Session of the Central Executive and Supervisory Committee continued to be held at the First Conference Hall of the Central Party Headquarters at 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 2nd. The attending committee members included Dai Jitao, Chu Minyi, Chen Guofu, Chen Lifu, Ding Chaowu, Enhe Batu, He Chengjun, Miao Bin, Yang Shuzhuang, Zhou Qigang, Liu Zhi, Gui Chongji, Wang Zhengting, Fang Juehui, Ding Weifen, Shao Lizi, Liu Jiwen, Zhang Qun, Chiang Kai-shek, Soong Tzu-wen, Liu Wendao, Lu Diping, Shao Yuanchong, Yu Youren, Liu Luyin, Ye Chucang, Zhu Jiahua, Zhang Daofan, Zhang Zhen, Chen Zhaoying, Kong Xiangxi, Yu Jingtang, Zeng Yangfu, Cheng Tianfang, Chen Bulei, Miao Peicheng, Wu Jingheng, Cai Yuanpei, Zhang Ji, Zhang Renjie, Ke Xing'e, Jiao Yitang, and Wu Tiecheng. Zhang Xueliang attended as an observer. Yu Youren chaired the meeting and passed two proposals for the National Assembly: (1) Determining the Trend of Educational Facilities. (2) Program for Industrial Construction.

Also on the 1st, the Central Provisional Plenary Session submitted two reports from the Central Standing Committee: one reporting that Fang Zhenwu had been expelled from the party for one year, and the vacancy would be filled by Kong Xiangxi, requesting it be filed for record; the other reporting that the selection of party representatives to attend the National Assembly by the provincial and military district party headquarters had been completed one after another, except for a small number of places for which official reports had not been received, and the list of representatives who had been elected was submitted for verification.

Central Proposals to the National Assembly

The Central Party Headquarters of the Kuomintang proposed a total of eighteen items to the National Assembly, listed as follows: (1) Plan for the annual construction of important railways and their ancillary projects. (2) Plan for the development of national highways with state subsidies. (3) Request for the determination of raising funds to clear the Jiaoji Railway bonds. (4) Raising funds to redeem the Chinese Eastern Railway. (5) Proposal on developing agriculture and improving the lives of farmers. (6) Proposal to establish model reclamation areas while stipulating forestry construction. (7) Implementing policies to encourage and protect industry. (8) Determining the direction of commercial development. (9) Promoting direct foreign trade. (10) Mining construction proposal. (11) Diplomatic strategy proposal. (12) Formulating a national hydropower generation and water storage irrigation program to promote the development of agricultural and industrial enterprises. (13) Implementing labor policies to promote the welfare of workers and promote industrial and commercial development. (14) Developing the natural gas industry. (15) National agricultural extension implementation plan. (16) Developing animal husbandry. (17) Improving the fishing industry. (18) Rectifying officialdom. In addition to the above eighteen proposals, there is also a capital construction proposal. As a result of the discussions at the Provisional Plenary Session on the 1st, it was decided that the capital construction proposal did not need to be submitted, and the remaining proposals were referred to a committee of nine, including Wu Jingheng, for review. The review committee began its review at the Central Party Headquarters on the morning of the 2nd and submitted a report to the General Assembly that afternoon.

Torrential Floods in the Three Rivers of Guangdong

▲The Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway Line Flooded

▲Huizhou and Shaozhou City Become a Land of Lakes

▲Qingyuan and Shixing Send Telegrams Requesting Relief

Guangzhou Dispatch: Due to continuous spring rains over the past month in Guangdong Province, the eastern, western, and northern rivers have simultaneously experienced torrential floods. On the East River, the Guangzhou-Kowloon railway line has already been submerged in several places. On the 24th, the first express train from Guangzhou to Shenzhen, traveling to the Gaomenlou Bridge No. 95 in Shilong, found that the bridge was submerged. The train was forced to return to Shilong, and traffic from the province to Shenzhen was disrupted again for several days. It is reported that the floodwaters continue to rise in the submerged areas. The East River flows through the lower reaches, but the flooding in the upper reaches is even more severe. The towns and cities along the banks of the upper East River have become a land of lakes, with many houses collapsing. Hengli and Tonghu in Huiyang, Paiwei, Qinü Lake, Sucun, and Shiwan in Boluo, and Qiaotou, Tiejang, Dongan, and Xianan in Dongguan are all submerged. Many houses in mountain villages near Henghe were destroyed by the floods from Mount Luofu, and many people drowned. A telegram from Shilong, Dongguan, reported yesterday that Shilong City and nearby areas are suffering from flooding. Low-lying areas are submerged up to the chest, and high-lying areas are submerged up to the knees. The water on the roads is more than three feet deep. Dikes in nearby villages have collapsed. Urgent relief is requested. At present, various charitable halls and business associations have discussed relief measures and will send personnel carrying over 16,000 catties of rice, over 20 loads of cakes and snacks, and medicine by train to the Shilong area for relief. The river near Huizhou has also become a vast expanse of water. The city and its suburbs are completely submerged. People travel on the streets by small boats. From the Clock Tower in the city to Datie Lane, the water is six feet eight inches deep. The streets along the upper and lower West Lake are about eight feet to one zhang deep. From Henglang Lane to Daxi Gate, the depth is over seven feet. From Daxi Gate to Fuxiang in the west of the city, the depth is over five feet. The water in the Xiami Street area near the Great East Gate is over one zhang deep, and the water in the upper and lower Tang areas is four to six feet deep. All schools have been completely suspended, shops have closed, and the poor are struggling to make a living. Charitable organizations have been organizing road repairs for days, providing work as a form of relief. On the West River, the originally constructed sluice gate in San Shui Luba, which cost over 100,000 yuan, was recently overwhelmed by the floodwaters. The floodwaters rushed back and flooded the villages on the opposite bank, turning them into a land of lakes. No less than dozens of houses have collapsed, and many residents have fled, resulting in numerous deaths. The ferry fare, which is normally only ten cents, has increased to two yuan. Since the 25th, the water level has risen further, making it impossible to cross the river. The villages along the Jiang'an coast have become a vast expanse of water. On the North River, mountain torrents are also raging. A section of the Ma-Ba railway track above Yingde was damaged by the flood, and Guangzhou-Shaozhou trains were suspended for several days before resuming operations yesterday. However, the water level in the Xiangjiang River in Qingyuan is still high. Dozens of boats have capsized in recent days. Because Qingyuan is located in the Xiangjiang River basin, when the North River rises, the Xiangjiang River also floods. Qingyuan County is the first to be affected. The disastrous situation is evident. Houses are collapsing and dikes are breached every day. Yesterday, the county reported that the water level in the county is rising rapidly, and all foundations are in danger. Efforts are being made to rescue the area, as the disaster is reminiscent of the Yimao year. The county is allocating funds to provide relief, but the disaster area is vast, and the resources are insufficient. Urgent relief funds are requested and await orders. In Shaozhou City, the water level was most turbulent on the morning of the 22nd. The streets in the city have become a land of lakes, with water depths exceeding four feet in higher areas and seven feet in lower areas. Many refugees have climbed onto rooftops to avoid the floodwaters. Police officers are using boats to rescue them. Those who have no homes are being provided with porridge by charitable organizations. The disaster situation in Shixing is also extremely serious. The county has also sent a telegram requesting relief. (28th)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

The Civil Education Hall Jointly Launches Health Propaganda: The Civil Education Halls of all counties in Jiangsu Province will jointly hold a health exhibition in Songjiang for three days, starting from the 13th of this month. An athletic meet will be held on the 15th, and a lantern parade will be held by all sectors in the evening. The City Health Movement Committee here has convened all members through the First District Office to prepare health slogans and banners in advance, which will be distributed to shops and residents along the area from Malu Bridge East to Puzhao Temple Bridge to be hung uniformly during the exhibition period. The committee has sent a letter to the Chamber of Commerce to request all shops to add small seals of slogan phrases on wrapping paper to attract customer attention and to prepare lanterns to participate in the lantern parade. It has sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau's First District Office to ban open-air pit toilets and food stalls, to cover food with gauze, and to urge hotels and inns to keep their bedding clean. The First District Office will plant cowpeas at the exhibition site to prevent epidemics, and draft industry books, slogans, and posters for selective display. The Education Bureau has also scheduled to convene representatives from various agencies and local figures on the 2nd to discuss the layout and reception matters. All staff of the Civil Education Hall are also preparing various health exhibition achievements, and a grand occasion is expected at that time. A Reactionary Criminal is Tried by a Provisional Court: Wu Qinghe, a counter-revolutionary criminal arrested in this county last year, was sent to the Suzhou Higher Court for trial. The county government has now received an order from the Higher Court stating that the Emergency Punishment Law for Endangering the Republic of China has been promulgated and implemented by the Ministry. Those who commit crimes stipulated in this law will be tried by a provisional court organized by the county magistrate and judicial officers in the bandit suppression area. Zhao and Deng, two judges from the Shanghai District Court, have been specifically appointed to come to Songjiang on a scheduled date to organize a provisional court to try the criminal. The police are also instructed to bring the criminal back. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Jin has complied by dispatching political police to Suzhou to escort the criminal and sending a letter to Shanghai to invite Judges Zhao and Deng to Songjiang to organize a provisional court for trial to reach a verdict.

The County Court Burns Opium: The county court has accumulated a large amount of opium pipes and opium confiscated from opium prohibition cases. Therefore, this afternoon (the 2nd), it was burned publicly in the square outside the court. The Higher Court was requested in advance to send personnel to supervise, and various agencies in the city participated. The Higher Court commissioner arrived in Songjiang by early train this morning and returned to Suzhou after completing the task.

Suzhou

Transfer of Three Prison Wardens: Ding Lei, the warden of the Third Prison Branch on Siqian Street and concurrently the director of the Higher Court Detention Center, has been ordered to switch positions with Chen Zhen, the director of the Lion's Mouth Temporary Shelter. The transfer was completed yesterday. After Chen Zhen took office, he immediately gave instructions to the detainees in the prison. The vacancy left by Ding Lei, who also served as the security director, has been filled by Zhang Jiechen.

Shanghai Detectives Seize Guns and Ammunition in Suzhou: On December 24th of last year, during a robbery at the home of a certain Mr. in No. 51, Shanxi Road, Shanghai, the criminal Zhou Asan confessed to hiding a handgun outside Qimen in Suzhou. Yesterday (the 2nd), detectives Wang Debiao and Deng Shu from the court were dispatched to Suzhou to join the Public Security Bureau, bringing Zhou, to recover a five-inch Browning pistol and eleven bullets from a grave mound in Anqian outside Qimen. The items were taken back to Shanghai.

Higher Court Transfers Three Judges: Cai, a judge of the Shanghai District Court, resigned, and his vacancy was filled by Wang Run, a judge of the Wuxian District Court, transferred by the Higher Court. Wang's vacancy was filled by Ling Yizhong from Wujin, and Ling's vacancy was filled by Liu Jinrong. In addition, Huang Zhixiao, a judge of Wuxian, resigned, and his vacancy was filled by Xuan Kai, a candidate judge of the Wuxi County Court. Xuan's vacancy was filled by You Changchen.

Changshu

A Murder Case Outside Ximen Takes an Unexpected Turn: The suspicious death case of Shen Fugen outside Ximen in this county was initially examined by the county and found to have claw marks. The family of the deceased, dissatisfied with the findings, appealed to the county party headquarters for relief. Shen Zuguang, a member of the Party Committee, went to the county to investigate and requested a re-examination, which led to a second examination. Now, students Feng Weifu, Yao Yuren, Zhou Yuchun, He You, and others from the Shanghai College of Politics and Law believe that Party Committee member Shen Zuguang interfered with the judiciary and violated the law, and have filed a complaint with the provincial government. After approval, the county has been ordered to investigate and verify the matter. Meanwhile, Feng and others have published a statement in the newspaper questioning three points of error in the "New Life Daily" published by the Party Headquarters.

Wuxi

The Grand Occasion of the May 1st Commemoration: Yesterday was the May 1st Commemoration Day. The workers in the city held a meeting at 9 a.m. in the city park, attended by tens of thousands of workers, laborers, and students. Wang Ciqing presided over the meeting. The entire group paid their respects, and speeches were given by Hui Jizhi, Pan Zhongjia, Zhang Hantian, and others. Proposals were passed, slogans were shouted, and photos were taken before the meeting adjourned. Immediately afterward, the police team set off on a parade to the train station, where they dispersed. The proposals passed are recorded below: ① Demand the implementation of the eight-hour system. ② Demand the revision of the Trade Union Law. ③ Demand the revision of the Factory Law. ④ Demand the issuance of revolutionary commemorative days to trade unions. ⑤ Demand the implementation of worker unemployment insurance. On this day, the security of the entire city was maintained by the review of the military police team and the business community, which was quite effective.

A Red Bandit is Escorted Back to Wuxi: The Red Bandit Jiang Zhenglin is from Huangmei Jia Mountain in this county. He has held various important positions in the bandit party. After being confirmed by former bandit party members Yan Fu and others, he was wanted by the provincial government. Recently, the county party and government agencies, based on a tip-off that the bandit Jiang Zhenglin was hiding in Huazang Temple in Kunshan, dispatched Committee Member Ji from the County Party Rectification Committee to Kunshan to cooperate with the Kunshan Public Security Bureau to arrest him. Jiang Zhenglin and Zhou were arrested on the spot and handed over to the Kunshan County Government for temporary detention. Yesterday, County Magistrate Pan sent police officers to Kunshan to escort them back to Wuxi with an official document. The court immediately opened to interrogate the two criminals, Jiang and Zhou, who both admitted to working for the Red Bandit Party without denial. After the interrogation, they were ordered to be returned to custody for further review.

A Ferry Sinks, Narrowly Avoiding Tragedy: In the 15th district (Qingcheng) of the county, there is a ferry at Yangcang Ferry, south of Gaojiajian, which operates daily and is very profitable. Yesterday, a temple fair was held in Fudan Village in the district, and villagers went to Tiangao City Yanshi Bridge to burn incense, attracting many villagers to watch. The ferry was overloaded, carrying as many as eighteen men and women. Unexpectedly, when it reached the middle of the river, it could not bear the weight and suddenly sank. At that time, the male and female passengers all became drenched chickens. They were rescued with great effort and were saved from drowning, which was fortunate.

Changzhou

Bandits Arrested in the Cuiqiao Robbery Case: Xu Zhang's family near Cuiqiao Town in Wu County was robbed a few days ago (the 29th). Zhu Miao, a patrol officer from the town's Public Security Substation, led the police and the business community to investigate and arrest a bandit named Qian Gengsheng, who was involved in the case. Local residents reported that the criminal was also involved in the major robbery and injury case at Ding Rurong's house in the 17th year. Officer Zhu considered the case to be related to bandits and immediately sent him to the Public Security Bureau in the city for interrogation on the 30th.

Nantong

A Bandit in Si'an Sentenced to Death: Dai Dashuang, a bandit in Si'an, was sentenced to death after being apprehended by the police and business community for robbery and murder.

Sea Bandits in Juegang Have Been Defeated: Sea bandits who were causing trouble in the Lvsi Sanjia Town area were suppressed by the armed fishing fleet and fled to Juegang. On the 20th, they were surrounded and suppressed by the 282nd Regiment, the Provincial Security Team, and the Water Police Team, sinking several bandit ships. The bandits fled towards Cha and are being pursued.

Unexpected Developments in the Daiwa Wheel Corpse Discarding Case: The court is investigating the Daiwa Wheel ship corpse discarding case. Recently, unexpected developments have led to mutual defamation lawsuits among the press and implicated Chief Prosecutor Zhu. The court has reported the situation to the Higher Court for verification.

A Bandit from Zhendao Was Captured in Tong: Tang Xiaodong, a bandit from Zhendao on the Tong-Ru border, was captured by the police team in Tong. Two Mauser pistols and sixteen bullets were seized and handed over to the county government for interrogation.

Rugao

A Rape and Murder Case Occurs in Xiyaojia: In Xiyaojia Garden, Baipu District, this county, there is a Zhu Yazi who has been in an illicit relationship with a widow surnamed Deng in the township for a long time. However, the widow recently had an affair. Zhu Yazi became extremely jealous and strangled her to death with a white cloth while she was sleeping on the night of the 25th of this month and fled. The next day, her biological mother noticed and rushed to report to the Public Security Bureau. After receiving the report, Director Yin immediately went to investigate with the township chief. He ordered the township officials to issue a guarantee for supervision and reported to the county government to send personnel for inspection.

Ningbo

Fire Outside Ximen: Yongfeng Sugar Mill, which has been operating for many years at Shiqiaotou Middle Street outside Ximen in Ningbo, caught fire around 2 a.m. today (the 30th) due to a stray match near a pile of firewood. The fire spread rapidly. Firefighters rushed to the scene and extinguished the fire after an hour. However, it had already spread to neighboring stores, including Fan Yuankang Clothing Store, Zhang Yonghe Chopstick Store, Lao Shunxing Cloth Store, Wang Yuanxing Firewood Store, and others, causing a total loss of more than 2,000 yuan.

Japanese Ship Sinks Fishing Boat: Lin Guangyu from Shenjiamen, Dinghai, makes a living by fishing. A few days ago, while he was fishing in the waters off Mount Yu, a Japanese ship sped by. The fishing boat was unable to avoid it and was hit amidships and sunk. Fortunately, the fishermen jumped into the sea and were saved from drowning by the Japanese ship. After the accident, the Japanese ship not only did not take responsibility but even tried to throw the fishermen into the sea. The fishermen cried for help, and another fishing boat heard their cries and came to the rescue. The fishermen were saved. The loss of the fishing boat is estimated to be over 1,000 yuan.

Shangyu

Frequent Robberies in the Songxia District: Gu Yungui's family near Zhutou Bridge, Ershe, Hutian, Songxia, was broken into by five or six unarmed bandits during a heavy rain the other night. They searched as they pleased, stealing 50-60 silver dollars and several rain gear items. They then went to Sun Dingkang's house, frightening the owner into silence, went upstairs, and plundered valuables. The losses are unknown. The bandits were still not satisfied and broke into Sun Xitang's house next door, taking away many soft items and clothing, resulting in a loss of more than 300 yuan. Xiang A'yi's family in Beixiangjia Village was also visited by six bandits with blackened faces and sharp blades, who stole a total of more than 600 yuan.

A Convicted Robber Jumps into the River During Transportation: Jin Jingkui, the owner of Jin Wenxing Iron Shop on Chengnan Street in the city, was arrested for robbing Xu Chen's pearl bag and hat on Chaihangdao Road near the city at the end of January. He refused to accept the county government's verdict and appealed to the Higher Court. The court summoned all parties involved for trial, and the result was that the original sentence of four years was upheld and increased to eleven years. He was to be escorted back to his place of origin for execution. However, Jin suddenly had a suicidal thought. On the 25th, while being escorted from Shaoxing to Yu, he jumped into the Baitayang River outside Dongguan. He disappeared in an instant. The escorts were unable to do anything and returned to Shaoxing to report to the District Court, which then reported to the Higher Court for verification.

Anqing

The Final Results of the Anhui Provincial General Election: The Anhui Provincial People's Assembly election has concluded, and the representatives of various groups will be officially announced on May 1st. The elected representatives are listed below: Education Association: Yang Zhongming, Cheng Binyi, Ye Jialong; Farmers' Association: Xia Futang, Wang Peizhen, Wang Jiyi; Labor Union: Chen Zhuofu, He Zhengtang, Chen Honghai; Chamber of Commerce: Zhang Zhaosen, Liu Zhang, Tao Yutang. The party member representatives are Wang Jianjin, Wei Kun, and Wu Qiyun.

Page 11

Education News

Sports

The 4th Jiangsu Provincial Inter-School Athletic Meet for Secondary Schools – Days 1 and 2

Parade Opening... Wu, Director of the Sports Field, Sworn into Office

Seven New Records Have Been Set, Suzhou Middle Schools for Boys and Girls Lead

Track and Field Finals Conclude Today, Ball Game Finals and Closing Ceremony Tomorrow

The 4th Jiangsu Provincial Inter-School Athletic Meet for Secondary Schools opened on the 1st. After the new rain, the weather was clear and warm, and everyone felt refreshed. In the past two days, a total of seven new records have been set in the track and field events for boys and girls. The ball games have also progressed from the preliminary rounds to the semi-finals. Today, the semi-finals of seven ball games for boys and girls will be held, and the situation is tense. The situation in the past two days is as follows:

Meet Overview

Pleasant Weather: The heavy rain stopped in the evening of the 30th. The 1st was suddenly bright and sunny, and the 2nd was the same. The weather was suitable for the events. After the new rain, both the competitors and the audience felt especially refreshed and comfortable.

Large Audience: Starting from the afternoon of the 1st, the audience was very crowded. It was estimated that thousands of people surrounded the field, and the hills to the left of the field were also filled with spectators. Yesterday was even more crowded than the 1st.

Well-Maintained Order: The order of the meet was very well-maintained. The 3rd Brigade maintained order. Even news reporters were not allowed into the field; only one photographer was allowed.

Scouts and Guides: The scouts and guides from the Zhenjiang Provincial Middle School took care of delivering messages and maintaining order in the field, which was extremely helpful.

Girls' School Performances: Girls' schools performed on both the 1st and 2nd. The Zhenjiang Girls' Vocational School was particularly praised by the audience on the 2nd for their neat, agile, and beautiful movements.

Provincial Doctors and Nurses: During the competition, doctors and nurses from the Zhenjiang Provincial Hospital were present to provide medical care. For example, in the girls' 80-meter hurdles, one girl fell after hitting a hurdle mid-race and was treated by them.

Director Sworn In

At 8 a.m. on the 1st, before the opening of the meet, the opening ceremony of the Provincial Sports Field was held. Director Wu Bangwei of the Sports Field was also sworn into office at the same time. Representatives from various agencies and the three commissioners, Hu, Sun, and Chen, from the provincial government attended. Commissioner Chen Hexian administered the oath, and the ceremony was held. Director Wu read the oath and reported on the preparations. The oath administrator Chen Hexian and provincial government commissioners Hu Pu'an and Yang Hongzhe gave speeches. Representatives from various agencies also gave speeches. Finally, Director Wu responded, music was played, and photos were taken. The ceremony concluded.

Parade Opening

At 9:30 a.m. on the 1st, Director-General Wu Bangwei reported on the opening ceremony. All the staff and athletes first paraded around the field once. The athletes from various schools wore bright costumes and marched in neat steps. Then, the athletes stood around the podium, and the scouts and guides held a flag-raising ceremony. After the ceremony, Chairman Chen Hexian delivered a speech, hoping that all students in the province would pay attention to sports and set an example for the public. He also hoped that the athletes would set new records in this province, gain a place in the national games to be held in the capital this year, and strive for the Far Eastern Games in the future. Yu Qingtang reported on the number of schools and athletes participating in this meet, and that their achievements surpassed previous meets. Director Hu gave a speech, generally saying that he expected good results. Niu Yongjian gave a speech, saying that the promotion of sports was essential to achieving world unity. Representatives from the provincial party headquarters, Qi Xiyong, the Jiangsu Pacification Supervisor, Li Tangshi, and the principals of the provincial schools of Suzhou Middle Schools, etc. successively gave speeches. After the ceremony, the games began.

Scoring Method

The scoring method for the meet is slightly different. In the track and field B group, no separate awards are given. Each school adds the scores of its A and B groups to calculate the total score. The school with the highest score wins the field or track championship because it is a unit. Relay races scores are doubled, and the remaining take a five, three, two, one scoring system.

Lu Xueqin's Illness

Suffering from a Stomach Ailment | Diligently Participated

Lu Xueqin of Songjiang Girls Middle School was bedridden for seven days before coming to the province and could not eat. The school advised her not to participate, but she insisted. Therefore, her results were not as good as the previous meet. Lu suffers from stomach problems.

Preliminary Rounds of Ball Games

Men's Soccer

Provincial Beijing Middle School Wins Against Private Yangzhou Middle School | Three to Zero

At around 9 a.m. on the 2nd, Provincial Nanjing Middle School competed against Provincial Yangzhou Middle School in soccer. Referee was Tang Zhongguang. Beijing Middle School's soccer skills were indeed stronger than Yangzhou Middle School's. Therefore, even though Beijing Middle School was in a downwind position in the first half, they were still able to kick in one goal. The ball was kicked in by Chen Hong. Although the Yangzhou Middle School goalkeeper caught the ball, it had already crossed the line. The referee thus ruled that Yangzhou Middle School lost one goal. In the second half, the sides were switched, and with the benefit of the tailwind, Beijing Middle School's ball control became even more intense. Yangzhou Middle School's area was filled with Beijing Middle School athletes, and they were penalized for corner kicks more than ten times, creating a one-sided situation. During this time, both corner kicks were kicked by Chen Hong and Tang. One landed in the right corner of the Yangzhou goal and was headed in by Yu Ren; the other was kicked in by Chen alone, which was extremely skillful. In conclusion, with a score of three to zero, Beijing Middle School won.

Men's Basketball

Provincial Suzhou Agricultural Wins Against Private Yangzhou Middle School

| Fifty-three to Twenty-one |

The preliminary round of the basketball match between Provincial Suzhou Agricultural School and Private Yangzhou Middle School resulted in a score of fifty-three to twenty-one. Referee was Shao Ji. Suzhou Agricultural occupied an extremely advantageous position. Its technique was far superior to that of Yangzhou Middle School. In the first half, Suzhou Agricultural scored twenty-two points, while Private Yangzhou Middle School scored eleven points. In the second half, Suzhou Agricultural continued to be strong, scoring thirty-one points, while Private Yangzhou scored ten points. The result was fifty-three to twenty-one. Suzhou Agricultural's left forward, Gao Xiaoda, scored twenty-five points, and right forward, He Qiruo, scored nineteen points.

Provincial Wuxi Middle School Wins Against Provincial Taicang Middle School

| Fifty-six to Twenty-four |

Provincial Wuxi Middle School and Provincial Taicang Middle School then battled. The situation was the same as the previous group. Wuxi Middle School's performance was very compact, and their strength was not bad. The result was fifty-six to twenty-four points. Referee was Jin Zhaojun. In the first half, Provincial Wuxi Middle School scored thirty-one points, while Taicang Middle School only scored seven points. In the second half, the situation did not diminish. As a result, Wuxi Middle School scored another twenty-five points, while Taicang only added seventeen points. Provincial Wuxi Middle School's right forward, Gu Yunqing, scored twenty-seven points alone.

Provincial Beijing Middle School Wins Against Nanjing Middle School

| Eighty-one to Twenty-six |

Beijing Middle School and Nanjing Middle School was another one-sided situation. Nanjing had no resistance. As a result, Beijing Middle School won by a large margin with a score of eighty-one to twenty-six. Referee was Wu Bangwei. Beijing Middle School's performance was exceptionally brilliant and had a good chance of winning the championship. The forwards cooperated very well, and the defense used a five-man defense. Nanjing did not know what to do. In the first half, Beijing Middle School scored thirty-nine points, and Nanjing scored five points. In the second half, Beijing Middle School scored forty-two points, and Nanjing scored eleven points. Beijing Middle School's right forward, Sun Lin, scored forty-three points alone.

Provincial Zhenjiang Middle School Wins Against Private Wuxi Middle School

| Forty-nine to Twenty-five |

This was the last battle of the first day's preliminary round, and it was fought in the twilight. The result was forty-nine to twenty-five. Zhenjiang Middle School won. Referee was Feng Jiasheng. Zhenjiang Middle School was exceptionally fierce. Private Wuxi Middle School's individual performance was also very good, but it was a pity that it lacked connection and ultimately failed. It was very regrettable. In the first half, Zhenjiang Middle School scored twenty-nine points, and Wuxi Middle School scored thirteen points. In the second half, Zhenjiang Middle School scored twenty points, and Wuxi Middle School only scored twelve points, which was of no avail and was eliminated.

Victory of Suzhou Girls' High School over Xuzhou Girls' High School

Twenty-one to Twenty

The Suzhou Girls' High School basketball team has consistently been a leader in provincial school athletic meets. Their shooting and passing are extremely accurate. The Xuzhou Girls' High School is physically strong and has a strong fighting spirit. After the start of the game, Suzhou Girls' High School had smooth sailing, leading in the first half with a score of eleven to six. Initially, the second half was also smooth, but then the two sides fought fiercely, each committing many fouls, with Suzhou Girls' High School being penalized more often. This ultimately resulted in a tie of seventeen to seventeen. The representative of Suzhou Girls' High School suggested that, according to the precedent of last year's National Games, when the scores are the same, the number of shots made and the number of free throws should be used to determine the winner. The referees decided that a rematch was necessary. So, the two sides fought bravely, and the students on the field all

cheered wildly to support them. In the end, Suzhou Girls' High School won the right to the semi-finals with a score of twenty-one to twenty. Xuzhou Girls' High School suffered a narrow defeat by one point, and the officials reportedly wept bitterly, which was truly a display of a lack of heroism. The referee was Shao Ji.

Track and Field Competition of the Joint Sports Association of Private Middle Schools in Jiangsu and Zhejiang

Two Firsts for Soochow University

Team and Individual, Dong Shuzhao

Two New Records… Javelin…

Triple Jump

The 4th Sports Meeting of the 4th Joint Sports Association of Private Middle Schools in Jiangsu and Zhejiang was held at the China Athletic Field on the 2nd. The results were: first place in the team competition, Soochow University Affiliated Middle School, with a total of thirty-nine points; second place, Shanghai University Affiliated Middle School, with twenty-five and a half points; third place, Jinling University Affiliated Middle School, with twenty-two points; and fourth place, Taowu Middle School, with sixteen points. First place in the individual competition, Dong Shuzhao of Soochow University, with fifteen points, was awarded by Mrs. Leighton. Two new records were created at the closing ceremony: Liu Jiayu of Shanghai University Affiliated Middle School in the javelin, with 41.42 meters, and Wang Yongmin of Taowu in the triple jump, with 12.54 meters.

Scores of Each Team

Participants included more than 200 athletes from twelve schools, including Jinling, Soochow, Cuiying, Yancheng, Taowu, Shanghai University, St. John's, Minqiang, Qingxin, Xiuzhou, Zhijiang, and Huilan. Soochow University won the championship with thirty-nine points (a total of five first places, three second places, two third places, and one fourth place). Shanghai University was second with twenty-five and a half points, Jinling was third with twenty-two points, Taowu was fourth with sixteen points, St. John's was fifth with fifteen points, Yancheng was sixth with nine points, Zhijiang was seventh with eight points, Minqiang was eighth with six points, Qingxin was ninth with five points, Cuiying was tenth with four and a half points, Huilan was eleventh with three points, and Xiuzhou was twelfth with one point.

Overview of Results

Liu Jiayu of Shanghai University threw the javelin 41.42 meters, breaking the first record of 40.16.5 meters set by Wen Dingxin of Shanghai University. Also, Wang Yongmin of Taowu jumped 12.54 meters in the triple jump, breaking his own third record of 12.28 meters. These were the new records of this conference. Cheng Jinguang, a short-distance runner from Yancheng, did not participate in the 100-meter, 200-meter, and 400-meter finals due to a leg injury yesterday, so it was a pity that he could not compare with his own conference record created in the third conference. The remaining results were relatively faded, even compared with the first Shanghai Secondary School Joint Sports Meeting held recently by the Shanghai Education Bureau.

Starting June 1st

Decide to Start Vacation Early

The principals of Jiangsu Provincial Middle Schools held a general meeting at Zhenjiang Middle School yesterday (30th) at 9:00 AM. Attendees included Ren Zhongmin (Zhenjiang Middle School), Wang Xiacai (Huaiyin Middle School), Chen Shi (Huai'an Middle School), Chen Shu (Suzhou Women's Middle School, Yang Jingqing representing), Wang Diancun (Suzhou Middle School), Xue Qiaodong (Xuzhou Middle School, Yu Yu representing), Zheng Tonghe (Shanghai Middle School), Gu Zhongchao (Tai Middle School, Zheng representing), Zhou Xingbei (Yangzhou Middle School), Chen Jingzhi (Songjiang Middle School), Feng Limin (Fisheries), Zhang Xiaoru (Nanjing Middle School), Chen Gucen (Wuxi Middle School), Sun Jie (Huanghai Middle School), Fei Dasheng (Suzhou Women's Middle School, Zhou representing), and Liao Jianan (Wang representing). Wang Diancun was unanimously elected chairman. After the formalities, Ren Zhongmin first reported on the arrears of funds and the urgent need for funds in various schools. The following major issues were then discussed and resolved: 1. Proposal on how to seek relief if schools cannot be maintained due to three months of arrears in funding. It was decided to elect representatives to petition the provincial government and the administrative office to clear the arrears before the fourth month by May 25th, otherwise the principals would not be able to bear the responsibility and would have to start the vacation early from June 1st. 2. According to the letter from the Ministry of Finance on March 14th, the amount of land tax levied over three years averaged more than 320 yuan per year, while the educational funding budget for the 19th year only listed 2.78 million yuan, a difference of more than 400,000 yuan, etc. (The original letter can be found in the Provincial Government Gazette No. 703.) What is the truth and should an inquiry be made? It was decided to inquire during the petition for the above case and bring it to the attention of the Education Funding Committee to pursue the arrears. 3. Educational staff serving in the three provinces should have the opportunity to go abroad for study in order to learn from experience and seek progress, and the funding should be included in the Education Department's budget. It was decided to submit a request to the Education Department to add an item for study expenses, following the regulations for educational staff studying local education. 4. For each subject in schools with different natures, the funding for each grade level should be calculated on a single-track basis. For schools with school buildings divided into three courtyards, the funding should be increased in proportion to the two courtyards. It was decided to submit a request to the Education Department again to allow the inclusion in the preparation of the next year's budget. 5. Should the number of research meetings for each subject be stipulated? It was decided that the proposed resolutions should be reviewed by the association. (1) The regulations for each subject research association should be submitted to the association for verification. If there are any improprieties, the association may express its opinions. (2) Regarding the resolutions passed by each association, those that do not involve school administration should be reported to the principal by the teachers of the relevant subject for implementation. Matters related to publication should be encouraged by each school. (3) Resolutions related to the administrative issues of one school should be decided by the principal of that school. (4) Matters involving the administrative issues of all schools must be sent to the association for review and approval before implementation. (5) The subject research meetings should be divided into (A) Party Ideology and Society, (B) Chinese, (C) English, and (D) Natural Sciences. Each type should hold one meeting per year, and two subject research meetings should be held each semester. 6. Can the summer conference be initiated by the association? It was decided that the association should initiate the drafting of the summer conference regulations by Suzhou Middle School and the preparation of the venue by Shanghai Middle School, tentatively scheduled for Putuo. 7. The letter from the Joint Association of English Subject Conferences of Provincial Middle Schools requesting discussion of the regulations was decided to be (1) The Joint Association of English Subject Conferences should be changed to the English Subject Research Association. (2) Article 4, "annual term" should be changed to "per academic year." (3) One full-time director should be appointed for a term of one year. (4) The chairman of the standing committee in Article 4 should be changed to the full-time director, and the rest should be approved. 8. Proposal for the Chinese subject examination: (1) Suzhou Middle School should be responsible for setting the questions and drafting the test paper format, which will be sent to each school for self-administration. Two students from each school should be selected for both senior and junior high levels. (2) Suzhou Middle School should set a deadline for collecting the test papers selected by each school and invite three experts from outside the school to evaluate them by a certain date. (3) The scores graded by the three experts should be averaged, and five students should be selected for both senior and junior high levels. 9. Should a Party Ideology speech competition be held? It was decided to hold it in the fall. 10. It was decided that (1) Each school should report independently, but the Chinese and English subject research associations have already been established, and mathematics will also be established soon. These three are basic subjects with a lot of research material and should be responsible for collecting and compiling them separately. (2) Yangzhou Middle School should be responsible for collecting Chinese research materials, Suzhou Middle School should be responsible for collecting English research results, and Shanghai Middle School should be responsible for collecting mathematics research materials. All should be submitted to the department before May 20th.

After the above ten proposals were discussed, they went to the Education Department to meet with the director to report everything. In the afternoon of the 1st, they continued to discuss issues such as the organization of student self-government associations and will make some suggestions.

Local News

Talk by Jiang Zuobin

Requesting Leave to Return Home to Report on Diplomacy

Sino-Russian Conference is Considered Smooth

Soviet Russia's Efforts are Extremely Admirable

European Economic Panic is Extreme

Jiang Zuobin, the Minister to Germany, requested leave to return home some time ago and stopped briefly in Moscow on his way. On April 29th, he arrived in Dalian and took the Changchun Maru southward. The day before yesterday (1st), he arrived in port at 3:00 PM. Tang Liu, the director of the Foreign Affairs Office, and Minister Jiang's wife and daughter all went to the Huangpu Wharf to greet him. After landing, Jiang took a car to his private residence on Lafayette Road to rest. Our reporter interviewed him at his residence. The following is a record of his talk.

Observation of Soviet Russia

Jiang said that he left Berlin on March 15th and arrived in Moscow on the 17th. He was ordered to inspect the Soviet Russian Five-Year Economic Plan. The highest design committee of the Five-Year Economic Implementation Plan led him to visit and inspect. As a result, the Soviet Union's economic plan was truly amazing. The spirit of unity and struggle from top to bottom was especially commendable. The outline of the plan is that the people of the whole country save on food and clothing, sell the goods they produce abroad at extremely low prices, and then use the money they earn to purchase various machines to improve domestic production. It is expected that the results will be considerable in a few years.

Minister Jiang Zuobin and his wife (photographed by this newspaper)

Sino-Russian Conference

Jiang also said that he met with Representative Mo Dehui repeatedly in Russia. The Sino-Russian conference is progressing smoothly. Three meetings have been held, and the Eastern Railway issue is still being discussed. The restoration of diplomatic relations and commerce have not been mentioned. It is rumored that the central government ordered him to assist Mr. Mo in handling the negotiations, but this is not true. The responsibility for diplomatic negotiations lies with the specialist. Representative Mo is knowledgeable, hardworking, and meticulous, and is worthy of important responsibility.

European Situation

When the reporter asked about the recent situation in Europe, Jiang replied that the panic in the European economic world has reached its peak. Unemployment is increasing day by day. Although all parties are trying their best to seek remedies, there is no thorough solution plan. As for the talk that the Second World War is about to break out, it is actually just nervous talk. European society mostly regards our country as a country that is determined to reform and is emerging. However, the governments of various countries still adhere to their self-interest and maintain their consistent policies.

Returning Home to Report

This time, I returned home to ask the government for leave, on the one hand to report the situation abroad to the central government. At the same time, because I have been away from the country for a long time, I can also take this opportunity to understand the progress of various matters in the country. As for the affairs of the embassy, they are currently being handled by Liang Long, the secretary of the embassy. I will go to Beijing within a few days. As for when I will return to my post, it will all depend on the will of the central government.

Shigemitsu Aoi Returned to Shanghai Yesterday

The Future of Sino-Japanese Jurisdictional Negotiations

Developing Based on the Principle of Reconciliation

Shigemitsu Aoi, the Japanese Chargé d'Affaires in China, arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon at 2:30 PM on the Nagasaki Maru. Those who greeted him at the Huishan Wharf included the Japanese Consul General Murai and others. After landing, Shigemitsu went to the Japanese Consulate General to rest and then returned to his private residence at 79 Qiqi Road. After arriving in Shanghai, Shigemitsu spoke to Chinese and foreign reporters, saying that he arrived in Tokyo on the 24th of last month and contacted the Japanese government's foreign affairs officials. The Sino-Japanese jurisdictional negotiations were very busy. Finally, a basic plan was decided in a short period of time. New developments are expected in the jurisdictional negotiations. Sino-Japanese relations are close, and reconciliation is necessary. Future negotiations should be conducted based on this principle. Shigemitsu did not give a specific indication of when he would go to Beijing to renegotiate with Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting yesterday. According to Japanese sources, the basic conditions for the Tokyo government's decision to abolish jurisdictional negotiations are: (1) Establishing special courts in special areas such as Shanghai; (2) Excluding Manchuria and Mongolia; (3) Opening up the Chinese interior; (4) Effectively protecting the lives and property of Japanese residents in China.

In 1929, he was a Chinese representative to the International Chamber of Commerce held in the Netherlands. Lang Xingshi is from Sudan. He studied in the United States and obtained a Master of Philosophy degree. The Post Office Seeks Accurate and Swift Mail Delivery

Relying on the Full Cooperation of the Public Concerned

It is heard from the Shanghai Post Office that Shanghai's population is increasing daily, and many new buildings are being constructed (especially apartments). Therefore, accurate and swift mail delivery has become a real problem. The Post Office is committed to providing the public with excellent service to the best of its ability. However, to facilitate this important work, it is necessary to rely on the full cooperation of the public concerned. It is extremely difficult to process mail with incomplete or inaccurate addresses. Therefore, in addition to clearly writing the recipient's full name, all house numbers, street names, and building

Page 14

names, etc., and in the case of apartments, the room number or residence number, and the floor number, must be specified in detail. If it is a foreign language letter, adding the Chinese address can further guarantee accurate and swift delivery. Also, for private residences, it is best to install a mailbox on the front door or in the hallway, or to make a slit in the door, and it should be installed in an easily accessible location for the postman to facilitate delivery. Furthermore, commercial organizations or apartments should install mailboxes in a conspicuous location in the lobby or entrance, or provide one for each residence or room, or establish a dedicated mail collection point to be fully responsible for receiving all mail for the building. The postal authorities are very willing to offer their advice on which system and which style of mailbox are most suitable.

Joint Investigation of Factory Information

Three Government Agencies

Two Academic Organizations

Starting from the 6th

The Accounting Department, Statistics Bureau, and Ministry of Industry of the National Government, in order to understand the state of domestic industry so as to compile statistics and promote domestic goods, will first investigate the mechanical industry in Shanghai and then other provinces. The Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau also wants to investigate the factories in this city to compare with the survey of 1928, and the Institute of Transportation of Jiaotong University wants to study the transportation of industrial products. The China Economic Society wants to study the rise and fall of domestic and foreign goods. Therefore, the three government agencies and two academic organizations have jointly established a Shanghai Industrial Survey Joint Office on the third floor of 50 Beijing Road, using the same form for a widespread investigation. Each agency has assigned more than ten staff members to share the investigation duties, which can avoid the trouble of repeated investigations in the factories, and the government agencies can also achieve twice the results with half the effort. It is truly a win-win situation. All investigators will be issued investigation certificates with the official seal of the Director of the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau for identification, and a half-length photo of the individual will be affixed to it. It is now heard that they will begin their investigation on May 6th.
