Commercial News

Finance

A Glimpse of the Gold Market in the Past Two Days

▲ The price fluctuated greatly on the 1st, ending with a continued rise. The day before yesterday, May 1st, was the World Labor Day commemoration, so the Japanese newspapers were closed. The gold market was quite good, but it fluctuated from time to time, hovering around 750 taels. In the end, it continued to rise by 5 taels and 1 mace, because Hengxing Sheng actively bought in. In addition to covering their shorts, they have turned long. Therefore, the market opened with a rise of 749 taels and 5 mace. The overseas silver market also fell, and foreign exchange was reduced by half a level, and the internal market was also tight. Later, it rose to 52 taels. Afterwards, due to large investors tending to sell, it turned sharply downward, and the atmosphere deteriorated sharply, falling 7 taels. In the afternoon, it fell to 42 taels, but speculators chased and bought, and it continued to peak, reaching 53 taels and 5 mace, closing at 52 taels and 3 mace, but the difference between the pre and post market was 11 taels and 5 mace.

▲ Yesterday's reaction found a small drop of 7 taels. Yesterday, the 2nd, the price of gold weakened again, retreating into the 750 tael range, but there were no major changes, only fluctuating by a little over 5 taels. In the end, it fell back by more than 7 taels. Rumors continued to circulate, which was actually a reversal after several days of successive rises. There was not much trading in the market. As for overseas silver, there was a different trend: British fell and American rose, so the price of gold opened low. Later, there were slight twists and turns. Due to the shortage of remittance bills, at noon it was between 45 taels. In the afternoon, because it was Saturday, the market closed. Examining the state of the week, it was confusing and uncertain. The maximum price was 53 taels and 5 mace, and the minimum price was 28 taels and 9 mace, a swing of 24 taels and 6 mace. Counting all six days, it only rose by 4 taels, and large investors such as Hengxing had turned long. Specialized spot firms are short, and those hedging remittance bills are about to break even. Therefore, short orders are also gradually selling, and the amount of cash orders is not large. It is said that the opening price in early June fell by 3 taels and 8 mace, totaling 748 taels and 5 mace. Large silver bars have fallen by 3/16, forward 1/8, the price of silver has risen by 1/4, and private telegrams have also increased by 1/8, so the sentiment is downward. Then, Da Xing, Yongfeng, etc. all sold, and it fell from 49 taels to 6 taels, and HSBC sold British gold in June at 1325. Then it went back up by more than 2 taels due to Wanjing Shunli and short covering. At the time of the first order, it was 48 taels and 5 mace, but the sellers were tireless, and Yu Da, Qian Changxiang, etc. all sold, and it was immediately reduced by 4 taels. Other bonds, such as Disbandment Bonds, 1929 Customs Bonds, 1929 Philanthropic Bonds, and 20-year Cigarette Bonds, etc., saw their markets become more prosperous than before, with bustling buying and selling. It is estimated that the total turnover in the morning and afternoon exceeded 26 million yuan, breaking the new record set on one day at the end of last month. As for the price trends of various bonds on this day, rumors frequently circulated in the South, causing anxiety in the market. Large amounts of buying and selling occurred among various trading groups, leading to dramatic price fluctuations. For example, in the morning session, due to strong buying, prices soared. 20-year Cigarette Bonds rose by about three and a half yuan, and others rose by two or three yuan. However, the situation in the afternoon session differed significantly, with selling pressure exceeding buying. Various bonds then plummeted, with the downward momentum no less intense than the morning's rise. As a result of the day's rise and fall, prices slightly decreased compared to the end of last month.

Day Two: On this day, although 20-year Customs forward trading had started, it was temporarily suspended due to excessive price fluctuations. The tense situation of other bonds remained unchanged from the previous day. Internal Disbandment Bonds experienced the largest fluctuations, resulting in the highest trading volume. Other bonds such as 20-year Cigarette Bonds, 1929 Customs Bonds, 1929 Philanthropic Bonds, and Disbandment Bonds remained bustling. In the first session alone, trading reached over 8.6 million yuan, and the second session saw over 7.7 million yuan. The afternoon situation showed no signs of diminishing, and the intensity of bond price fluctuations remained as high as in the morning session. Market sentiment became increasingly weak, with selling becoming more prevalent. Prices of various bonds plummeted, making the market even more tense than in the past few days, with fluctuations of two or three yuan. In the afternoon, the selling pressure intensified, and the supply-demand imbalance widened. 1929 Customs Bonds, 1929 Philanthropic Bonds for the next month, 20-year Cigarette Bonds, and Whole Six Bonds for May delivery all experienced sharp declines and trading halts. Other bonds also fell by more than three yuan, but trading was halted as it approached 6 PM. It is estimated that the total forward trading volume for the day still reached 23 to 24 million, while spot trading was only ten thousand yuan.

Yarn and Cotton

The Yarn Market is Declining Rapidly

Yarn Market: The sharp decline in Shanghai caused rumors to spread in the market, weakening confidence. Buyers were panicked, and some bulls turned bearish. As a result, the market became increasingly weak. Sellers seized the opportunity to pressure the market, causing it to decline rapidly, resembling a river flowing downhill. However, one manufacturer vigorously purchased this month's yarn. Nevertheless, the prevailing trend was strong, and it was difficult to maintain independently. Spot yarn trading was reportedly sluggish, with various trading groups hesitant to act due to the adverse environment. In summary, the weakness in the global cotton market exerted pressure on the local market. Coupled with unsettling rumors, it was difficult to stabilize confidence. Therefore, large speculators shifted from bullish to bearish positions. The focus should be on the 152-153 tael range.

▲Man Biao Down Three to Four Taels: Man Biao opened in the morning session with a sharp drop in US cotton, causing panic. Bulls turned bearish, and prices for all months fell by two taels three qian to three taels. One manufacturer purchased this month's yarn, which fell by one tael one qian. The market sentiment remained weak in the afternoon, with many rumors circulating. Prices for all months fell by another one tael two qian six qian. Silk and Tea

Silk Market Sluggish for Two Days

The Shanghai foreign firm silk market continued its sluggish trend in the past two days. Due to economic instability in overseas markets, silk factories were focusing on artificial silk to reduce costs, and natural silk factories were unable to sell their products. Silk telegrams did not arrive. In the past two days, only Jardine Matheson and others purchased 20 bales of Shanghai white silk, Nadier and others purchased 35 bales of Sichuan yellow silk, and New Cheong Shing and others purchased 15 bales of white silk. Prices were generally weak.

Shaoxing Spring Silkworms Damaged by Cold Rain

▲The First Brood Completely Abandoned... The Condition of the Second Brood is Also Not Good

Farmers in various cities and villages in Shaoxing started to incubate silkworm eggs around the 10th of this month. Silkworms began to hatch successively after the 16th. However, the weather was extremely cold, and thunderstorms occurred during the first molt, causing silkworm diseases that resulted in the complete abandonment of the first brood. Silkworm farmers re-incubated a second batch of silkworm eggs, but the climate remained cold and rainy. Although the early silkworms have now entered the second molt, their development is unfavorable, and some have died. The condition is not good, and silkworm farmers are generally pessimistic.

Zhenmei Green Tea Plummets Again and Again

The local foreign firm tea market has been trending sparse lately, due to dwindling tea stocks. Yesterday, only Jardine Matheson, Fu, and other firms purchased over 200 boxes of Zhenmei from Yong Gao. The selling price has fallen to 63-64 taels, which is another 7-8 taels lower than before. Tunxi and Ying County teas have also fallen by 2-3 taels. The market situation is quite pessimistic.

Britain Levies Additional Import Tax on Chinese Tea

A telegram from London states that the British government, in order to increase foreign tax revenue, intends to levy an additional penny on the import tax of Chinese tea. It is understood that the British practice has been to levy a tax rate of six pennies per dan of Chinese tea. Now, it is proposed to change the levy to seven and a half pennies. The British government has formally submitted this proposal to the upper and lower houses for review and approval, and it will be implemented soon. According to current calculations, this will increase the cost by an additional twenty-five taels of Chinese silver per dan of tea, which will significantly affect the trade between Chinese tea and Britain.

Wenzhou New Green Tea Has Already Emerged

Wenzhou new green tea has emerged on various mountain peaks in recent days. Tea farmers, persuaded by tea merchants, have started picking early. The tea leaves that have emerged are quite tender. However, tea factories in the region have suffered significant losses in recent years, with six or seven fewer factories compared to the past. Due to tight credit conditions, most are adopting a passive approach. Although countryside traders had initially agreed to a starting price of 30 yuan per dan for new teas, this has not yet been confirmed.

Qimen Tea Market Opens at the Highest Record Price

Qimen black tea is generally considered to be best from the Western region, with the Southern region being slightly inferior. Last year, foreign merchants suddenly shifted their strategy, placing more emphasis on the Southern region. As a result, businesses in the Southern region gained more profits, while those in the Western region gained less. It is estimated that Qimen had the most successful black tea trade last year, while most other areas incurred losses. Therefore, this year, pawnshops are paying close attention to the Qimen tea market. Shanghai tea merchants and Qimen branches are also expanding the scope of their invitations and loans to Qimen tea merchants. The total amount loaned to Qimen businesses by various merchants is approximately one million yuan. Due to intense competition among tea merchants, tea farmers are raising mountain prices. Yesterday, the first batch released by tea farmers was priced from 100 yuan to 80 yuan per shipment. The cost of green tea leaves is over 200 yuan per dan, which is 30-40 yuan higher than before, representing the highest new record price for the Qimen tea market. Tea merchants are hesitant to purchase at these mountain prices and hope for lower prices to reduce costs. However, with market trends favoring higher prices, it is uncertain whether they will get their wish.

The Art World

Painting and the Modern Spirit

— Kang

The expression of art has two aspects: the vertical and the horizontal. The vertical descends from ancient history and legends, while the horizontal extends into the real life around us. In the current Chinese art scene, to discover a good work that possesses a modern spirit while not abandoning the beautiful legends of the past is as difficult as finding a spring in the desert. Many people therefore regard art as an ivory tower to escape the world, and in their works, they refuse to imbue them with their own real feelings towards the masses. The climate of the art world naturally becomes even more depressing and stifling. In recent years, due to domestic natural disasters and man-made calamities, as well as the chaos of war, people are too busy saving themselves to even inquire about art, which cannot satisfy hunger or provide warmth. Therefore, during this transitional period, the poverty of the Chinese art world is felt to be pitiful. However, there are also some who show some concern, while others are singing the high tune of "art for art's sake," seemingly completely unrelated to the hidden feelings and suffering of the people. The objective environment is ignored in their presence, making it even more difficult for artists in this situation to produce something that grasps the essence of the times.

This time, the Morning Light Art Society, with the spirit of opening up a barren land, has contributed a little bit of strength. The impact of this strength is an impression that we cannot erase: that is, from the vertical aspect, they can pay attention to the legends of their own nation, and from the horizontal aspect, they faithfully infuse their works with intense, brave, and tragic emotions. This is probably generally recognized.

We know that the tide of the times has surged to its highest point. The bloodshed of the May Thirtieth Movement created a vanguard for the national revolutionary history. People who were once wandering at the crossroads are now, due to the survival and competition of the nation, inevitably awakened. Their dreams of "art for art's sake" are shattered. Consequently, some who have recognized the true face of the times have joined the military to engage in actual struggle. The national revolution has gradually reached its final stage. The progress of the great era has clearly demarcated the boundary between the old and the new. The so-called tranquil and inactive life that artists once regarded as elegant has long been washed away by the flood-like tide. The world before us is a world where the entire nation rises up to struggle. The art that expresses the times is naturally no exception. On the one hand, in the withering garden, we see the leaves falling completely; on the other hand, we can see green filling the branches. In the temporary intersection of metabolism, artistic works that express national consciousness increasingly form the cutting edge of the times. The Morning Light Fifth Exhibition began to meet with people in society under such demands. Now, based on the analysis of the times and the transformation of our pace with the times, we are gradually seeing here that the output of this consciousness differs from that of other exhibitions.

Regarding the vertical aspect, there are folk legends. Legends are the product of experiential products. Due to different environmental relationships, each nation must have their different legends. China, known as the most outstanding and oldest nation, naturally has no shortage of legends from its ancestors, and they have been passed down to the people to this day. Our products related to this category include "The Sun Chariot," "Hou Yi Shooting the Sun," "Nüwa," "Cowherd and Weaver Girl," and "The Battle of Zhuolu," all of which are used as themes for the works as much as possible. In the painting "The Sun Chariot," we can also see the commonality of myths among nations. In ancient times, we had the legend of "Di Yu Yi He." However, this sun, which shines all over the world, can also be extracted from the Greek myth of Phaeton driving the sun chariot. It is said that the sun chariot fell in Africa and burned all their houses, and their bodies were scorched black, so they are always the color of charcoal ash. As for the legends about the relationship between the two sexes, there are also many in mythology. "Shooting the Sun" is an image of our ancient nation conquering nature. Hou Yi is said to be a brave and unparalleled man, and his wife Chang'e is also very beautiful. At that time, there were nine suns always arranged in the celestial bodies. Hou Yi used amazing strength to draw the bow and arrow and shoot one to illuminate the present sun. Second, Nüwa refined stones to mend the sky. This is because Nüwa saw that "the air in the sky was insufficient, so she refined colorful stones to fill the gaps..." As for the description of the Cowherd and Weaver Girl, it is purely a symbol of the love between men and women in ancient rural areas, and it also contains the meaning of encouraging cultivation and weaving. The legend of war is the story of the Yellow Emperor fighting against Chi You. At that time, the Han people moved into the Central Plains and fought fiercely with Chi You, the leader of the Miao people, in the wilderness of Zhuolu. In addition to being strong and fierce, Chi You could also make fog to confuse the Yellow Emperor's army. Therefore, the Yellow Emperor invented the compass chariot and overcame Chi You. This can more fully express the progressive and courageous spirit of our ancient nation.

Regarding the horizontal aspect, there are national humiliation and the facts of national struggle. Let us now try to open our eyes and see if the facts before us are enough to make us

Page 22

shocked and alarmed. The country is almost full of devastation as a result of years of warlord infighting, and it is again weighed down by the invasion of international imperial capitalism. A large China has almost been reduced to a semi-colonial status, which is even worse than that. The people, under successive tragedies, are also subjected to years of starvation. Those who do not die from bloodshed and bullets starve to death in ditches. The strong, however, take risks and become thieves and bandits. In the cities, there are also tragic incidents of humiliation. Anyone with a little feeling can make their heart ache for everything that is presented, especially in the seas where foreign forces are expanding. Because they are looking for a trading place, they do not hesitate to send many warships to transport strong military forces for protection. They run rampant at will in the concessions. Even the masters of this territory can only be trampled by others under the power of foreigners. May I ask, where did the tragedies occur? Isn't it in the concessions? Isn't every concession filled with foreign troops? In our products, this impression can be captured. In the "Shooting Range," they practice shooting there every day to prepare to attack us. This situation can be clearly seen. In addition, "What I Saw in Hongkou" blatantly highlights the Japanese imperialists. They display sharp armored vehicles there. The fierce gaze of the Japanese soldiers is always the same. When the National Revolutionary Army arrived in Shanghai, the French imperialists built many iron gates at the junction of the French Concession. The work titled "Iron Gate" reminds us of the imperialists' hatred of the Chinese nation. These humiliating works give us a sharp stimulus.

Now let us inspect the suffering of the people in the country. They have been suffering for a long time under the iron hooves of the warlords, unable to live and unable to die. This is worth sighing for. However, after the revolutionary forces flooded the north and south of the Yangtze River, the wheels of the times have gradually pushed them to awaken. In this great period of change, there are of course many traumas. After the war, they are still unavoidable from freezing and starvation, and even displaced and homeless. This situation is very easy to find in northern China. When we look at the two works "Displacement" and "Disaster Victims," the poems chanted by the ancients, "The fields are desolate after the war, and family members are displaced on the roads" and "The vermilion gates reek of meat and wine, but the roads have frozen corpses," become more sad and poignant.

The suffering of the Chinese nation, according to the current situation, is truly unprecedented. Historically, even the Hong Yang Rebellion was not as tragic as the current Red Disaster. This belongs to the events in southern China. In the works such as "Impression of Changsha" and "Red Terror," we can feel a pressing atmosphere. Many people's lives and many magnificent buildings were destroyed in the outbreak of fire and blood. The state of terror and turmoil still makes people shudder when they think about it. Other depictions of national struggle include works such as "Wild Rose," "Female Propagandist," and "Crossing the Yellow River at Dawn," "Meeting in Zhengzhou," and other works as representatives. In the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, the iron cavalry of the warlords wantonly roamed the provinces south of the Yangtze River, and the people were in deep water and scorching heat. The emotions of resistance had reached boiling point, especially the people of Zhuji County, Zhejiang Province. "Wild Rose" is the scene of the author capturing the people preparing to respond to the revolutionary army at that time. At that time, all the women used fierce emotions to encourage men to fight. The strong and healthy "Wild Rose" we saw is the typical of the women in that area. "Female Propagandist" is also a feeling of the female compatriots that the current national suffering is not only relying on the strength of men to completely achieve the victory of liberation. Therefore, their courage to participate in actual work is no less than that of Mulan in those years. As for the situation of the revolutionary army going out on expeditions, and the facts of the battles, we can realize the tension of military affairs in the war zone and the enthusiasm of the people's welcome in the misty "Crossing the Yellow River at Dawn" and the several works of "Meeting in Zhengzhou." Now, if you think about it a little bit, the blood wheels all over your body should also be boiling.

Therefore, these products not only have the description of grasping the cutting edge of the times, and the unique style and characteristics, but also give new life to art.

The Morning Light Art Exhibition was originally scheduled to close tomorrow. It is reported that the exhibition will be extended for three days until the 7th of this month. The venue is still at the Shanghai Art School at the intersection of Jiangwan Road and Tongji Road (Reporter's Note)

Manuscript Guidelines for the Art World

(1) The text is limited to news, reviews, and introductions about the latest art (painting, music, sculpture, architecture, drama, etc.) and literature at home and abroad.

(2) The photos are limited to the latest portraits and works of writers at home and abroad and various photographs related to the text.

(3) The number of words in each article should not exceed two thousand at most.

Do not write on both sides of the paper.

(4) Write horizontal characters in the manuscript, do not write sloppily. Western text should be omitted where possible. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached under the translation.
